<p>In
April
2009,
<a
href="/wiki/Phil_Griffin_(director)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Phil
Griffin
(director)">Phil
Griffin</a>'s
documentary
on
the
band,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/When_We_Were_Beautiful?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="When
We
Were
Beautiful">When
We
Were
Beautiful</a>&quot;,
debuted
at
the
<a
href="/wiki/Tribeca_Film_Festival?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tribeca
Film
Festival">Tribeca
Film
Festival</a>,
chronicling
Bon
Jovi's
ups
and
downs
over
25
years
and
following
the
band
on
their
latest
Lost
Highway
tour.</p>








<p>In
June
2009,
Jon
Bon
Jovi
and
<a
href="/wiki/Richie_Sambora?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Richie
Sambora">Richie
Sambora</a>
were
inducted
into
<a
href="/wiki/Songwriters_Hall_of_Fame?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Songwriters
Hall
of
Fame">Songwriters
Hall
of
Fame</a>.
That
month
they
also
recorded
a
cover
of
the
song
&quot;Stand
By
Me&quot;
with
Iranian
singer
<a
href="/wiki/Andy_Madadian?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Andy
Madadian"
class="mw-redirect">Andy
Madadian</a>,
to
show
solidarity
for
those
affected
by
political
unrest
in
Iran.
Parts
of
the
song
were
sung
in
<a
href="/wiki/Persian_language?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Persian
language">Persian</a>.</p>








<p>On
November
10,
2009,
the
band
released
their
11th
studio
album,
entitled
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Circle_(Bon_Jovi_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Circle
(Bon
Jovi
album)">The
Circle</a></i>.
The
Circle
is
a
return
to
rock
n'
roll
after
their
Nashville
influenced
album,
<i>Lost
Highway</i>.
The
album
debuted
at
number
one
in
the
US,
Canada,
Germany
and
Japan.
Bon
Jovi
headed
out
on
the
road
once
again
on
February
19,
2010,
embarking
on
<a
href="/wiki/The_Circle_Tour?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Circle
Tour">The
Circle
Tour</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-33"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-33"><span>[</span>33<span>]</span></a></sup>
Bon
Jovi
kicked
off
the
stadium
leg
of
the
Circle
Tour
by
making
history.
They
played
the
first
ever
show
at
the
brand
new
<a
href="/wiki/New_Meadowlands_Stadium?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="New
Meadowlands
Stadium"
class="mw-redirect">New
Meadowlands
Stadium</a>
in
East
Rutherford,
New
Jersey.
The
three
sold
out
shows
on
May
26,
27
and
29,
2010
were
a
huge
success.
Bon
Jovi's
12
night
run
at
London's
O2
Arena
grossed
$18,178,036
and
seen
them
play
to
187,696
fans.
The
Circle
Tour
was
the
highest
grossing
concert
tour
of
2010
according
to
Billboard's
annual
Top
25
concert
tours.
So
far
the
tour
has
played
to
1,909,234
fans
and
has
grossed
$201.1
million
from
more
than
80
venues
reported
to
Pollstar.<sup
id="cite_ref-34"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-34"><span>[</span>34<span>]</span></a></sup>
For
the
second
time
in
three
years,
Bon
Jovi
ranked
as
Billboard's
&amp;
Pollstar's
Top
Touring
Act
of
the
Year.
Bon
Jovi
was
also
ranked
second
on
<a
href="/wiki/Forbes_Magazine?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Forbes
Magazine"
class="mw-redirect">Forbes
Magazine's</a>
list
of
the
world's
highest
paid
musicians,
earning
an
approximate
$125
million
income
that
year.<sup
id="cite_ref-35"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-35"><span>[</span>35<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Bon
Jovi
released
a
greatest
hits
album
with
four
new
songs
in
October
2010.
The
album
debuted
at
number
one
in
Canada,
Ireland,
Europe,
Australia
and
made
the
top
five
in
twenty
countries.
At
the
<a
href="/wiki/2010_MTV_Europe_Music_Awards?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="2010
MTV
Europe
Music
Awards">2010
MTV
Europe
Music
Awards</a>,
Bon
Jovi
received
the
<a
href="/wiki/MTV_Europe_Music_Award_for_Global_Icon?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="MTV
Europe
Music
Award
for
Global
Icon">Global
Icon
Award</a>.
In
October
2010,
Bon
Jovi
released
the
concert
film,
&quot;The
Circle
Tour
Live
From
Jersey&quot;
in
U.S.
theaters.
At
the
same
time,
the
band
announced
their
upcoming
tour.
At
the
conclusion
of
2011,
the
tour
placed
second
on
Billboard's
annual,
&quot;Top
25
Tour&quot;,
earning
over
&pound;790
million
dollars.<sup
id="cite_ref-36"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-36"><span>[</span>36<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Inside_Out_and_What_About_Now_.282012.E2.80.93present.29"><i>Inside
Out</i>
and
<i>What
About
Now</i>
(2012–present)</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bon_Jovi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11"
title="Edit
section:
Inside
Out
and
What
About
Now
(2012–present)">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>In
January
2012,
Jon
Bon
Jovi
stated
that
they
were
working
on
a
twelfth
studio
album,<sup
id="cite_ref-37"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-37"><span>[</span>37<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
in
a
live
show
in
August
2012,
Jon
Bon
Jovi
played
an
acoustic
version
of
a
song
that
was
announced
to
be
on
the
upcoming
album.<sup
id="cite_ref-38"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-38"><span>[</span>38<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
October
2012,
Bon
Jovi
announced
<a
href="/wiki/Because_We_Can_(concert_tour)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Because
We
Can
(concert
tour)">Because
We
Can</a>,
a
new
world
tour
for
2013,
in
support
of
their
new
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/What_About_Now_(Bon_Jovi_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="What
About
Now
(Bon
Jovi
album)"
class="mw-redirect">What
About
Now</a></i>,
which
was
released
on
March
12,
2013.
The
tour
started
in
February
2013
and
visited
North
America,
Europe,
Africa,
the
Far
East,
Australia
and
Latin
America.<sup
id="cite_ref-BecauseWeCan_3-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-BecauseWeCan-3"><span>[</span>3<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>On
November
27,
2012,
Bon
Jovi
released
a
new
live
video
album,
called
<i><a
href="/wiki/Inside_Out_(Bon_Jovi_Album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Inside
Out
(Bon
Jovi
Album)"
class="mw-redirect">Inside
Out</a></i>,
made
up
of
content
from
shows
at
the
<a
href="/wiki/The_O2_Arena_(London)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
O2
Arena
(London)"
class="mw-redirect">O2
Arena</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/MetLife_Stadium?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="MetLife
Stadium">MetLife
Stadium</a>,
and
<a
href="/wiki/Madison_Square_Garden?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Madison
Square
Garden">Madison
Square
Garden</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-inside_out_39-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-inside_out-39"><span>[</span>39<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
album
was
first
shown
at
movie
theaters,
with
screenings
preceded
by
a
question-and-answer
session
with
Jon
Bon
Jovi,
Richie
Sambora,
David
Bryan
and
Tico
Torres
streamed
live
from
a
theater
in
New
York,
and
was
subsequently
made
available
for
purchase
on
<a
href="/wiki/ITunes?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="ITunes">iTunes</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-inside_out_39-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-inside_out-39"><span>[</span>39<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>On
March
14,
2013,
Bon
Jovi
appeared
on
the
results
show
of
American
Idol
and
played
one
song,
Because
We
Can,
from
their
new
album
What
About
Now.<sup
id="cite_ref-American_Idol_40-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-American_Idol-40"><span>[</span>40<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>From
2
April
forward,
Richie
Sambora
departed
the
band's
ongoing
tour
for
unspecified
&quot;personal
reasons&quot;;
Phil
X
once
again
replaced
him,
this
time
for
the
remainder
of
the
tour,
amidst
rumours
that
Sambora
had
been
fired.<sup
id="cite_ref-41"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-41"><span>[</span>41<span>]</span></a></sup>
Both
Sambora
and
Jon
Bon
Jovi
later
denied
the
claim.<sup
id="cite_ref-42"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-42"><span>[</span>42<span>]</span></a></sup>
Tico
Torres
was
also
sidelined
briefly
due
to
emergency
gallbladder
surgery;
he
was
replaced
by
Rich
Scannella
from
Bon
Jovi's
solo
band,
the
Kings
of
Suburbia,
from
20
September
to
6
October.<sup
id="cite_ref-43"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-43"><span>[</span>43<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Solo_projects">Solo
projects</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bon_Jovi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12"
title="Edit
section:
Solo
projects">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>During
the
band's
first
sabbatical
between
1990-1991
Jon
Bon
Jovi
recorded
a
solo
album,
a
soundtrack
to
the
movie
<i><a
href="/wiki/Young_Guns_II?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Young
Guns
II">Young
Guns
II</a></i>
more
commonly
known
as
<i><a
href="/wiki/Blaze_of_Glory?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Blaze
of
Glory">Blaze
of
Glory</a></i>.
Released
in
1990,
the
title
track,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Blaze_of_Glory_(Jon_Bon_Jovi_song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Blaze
of
Glory
(Jon
Bon
Jovi
song)">Blaze
of
Glory</a>&quot;
peaked
at
number
one
on
the
Billboard
Hot
100.
In
1991
&quot;Blaze
of
Glory&quot;
won
an
award
for
Favorite
Pop/Rock
Single
at
the
<a
href="/wiki/American_Music_Awards?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="American
Music
Awards"
class="mw-redirect">American
Music
Awards</a><sup
id="cite_ref-american-music-awards_2_44-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-american-music-awards_2-44"><span>[</span>44<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
awarded
a
<a
href="/wiki/Golden_Globe?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Golden
Globe"
class="mw-redirect">Golden
Globe</a>,
as
well.
The
song
also
earned
Jon
Bon
Jovi
an
<a
href="/wiki/Academy_Award?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Academy
Award"
class="mw-redirect">Academy
Award</a>
nomination
and
a
<a
href="/wiki/Grammy?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Grammy"
class="mw-redirect">Grammy</a>
nomination.</p>








<p>Richie
Sambora,
with
the
help
of
Tico
Torres
and
David
Bryan,
released
a
solo
album
entitled
<i><a
href="/wiki/Stranger_In_This_Town?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Stranger
In
This
Town"
class="mw-redirect">Stranger
In
This
Town</a></i>,
in
1991.
The
album
featured
<a
href="/wiki/Eric_Clapton?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Eric
Clapton">Eric
Clapton</a>
on
the
song
&quot;Mr.
Bluesman&quot;.
David
Bryan
recorded
a
soundtrack
for
the
horror
movie
<i>The
Netherworld</i>,
which
was
the
brighter
part
of
that
year
after
he
was
hospitalized
with
an
illness
caused
by
a
South
American
parasite.
Alec
John
Such
took
a
fall
off
of
his
motorcycle
which
injured
his
bass-playing
hand,
forcing
him
to
develop
a
whole
new
way
to
hold
and
play
his
instrument.</p>








<p>In
1997,
Jon
Bon
Jovi
landed
lead
roles
in
several
movies.
While
he
was
free
between
filming
different
movies,
Jon
wrote
what
would
become
his
second
solo
album,
1997's
<i><a
href="/wiki/Destination_Anywhere?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Destination
Anywhere">Destination
Anywhere</a></i>.
A
short
movie
of
the
same
name
was
recorded
around
the
record's
release,
based
entirely
on
the
songs
from
the
record
and
starring
Jon
Bon
Jovi,
<a
href="/wiki/Demi_Moore?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Demi
Moore">Demi
Moore</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Kevin_Bacon?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kevin
Bacon">Kevin
Bacon</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Whoopi_Goldberg?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Whoopi
Goldberg">Whoopi
Goldberg</a>.</p>








<p>Tico
Torres
used
the
opportunity
to
further
pursue
his
painting
while
David
Bryan
started
writing
and
composing
various
musicals.
In
1998,
Richie
Sambora
released
his
second
solo
outing
titled
<i><a
href="/wiki/Undiscovered_Soul?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Undiscovered
Soul">Undiscovered
Soul</a></i>.</p>








<p>In
2012,
the
band
members
embarked
on
solo
projects
once
again,
meanwhile
recording
their
<i><a
href="/wiki/What_About_Now_(Bon_Jovi_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="What
About
Now
(Bon
Jovi
album)"
class="mw-redirect">What
About
Now</a></i>.
Returning
to
film
composing
for
the
first
time
since
<i>Blaze
of
Glory</i>,
Jon
Bon
Jovi
wrote
and
recorded
two
songs
for
the
<a
href="/wiki/Al_Pacino?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Al
Pacino">Al
Pacino</a>
film
<i><a
href="/wiki/Stand_Up_Guys?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Stand
Up
Guys">Stand
Up
Guys</a></i>,<sup
id="cite_ref-45"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-45"><span>[</span>45<span>]</span></a></sup>
while
Richie
Sambora
recorded
and
released
his
third
studio
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Aftermath_of_the_Lowdown?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Aftermath
of
the
Lowdown">Aftermath
of
the
Lowdown</a></i>,
and
supported
it
with
a
short
world
tour
in
October
2012.<sup
id="cite_ref-46"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-46"><span>[</span>46<span>]</span></a></sup>
As
regards
Tico
Torres
he
focused
on
playing
golf,
by
taking
part
in
several
tournaments
and
being
captured
by
many
different
cameras
while
David
Bryan
made
a
short
performance
at
Fantiscritti,
<a
href="/wiki/Carrara?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Carrara">Carrara</a>
in
May
26,
2012.</p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Musical_style">Musical
style</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bon_Jovi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13"
title="Edit
section:
Musical
style">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>Bon
Jovi's
musical
style
has
generally
been
characterized
as
'<a
href="/wiki/Hard_rock?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Hard
rock">hard
rock</a>',
'<a
href="/wiki/Glam_metal?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Glam
metal">pop/hair
metal</a>',
'<a
href="/wiki/Arena_rock?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Arena
rock">arena
rock</a>'
and
'<a
href="/wiki/Pop_rock?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Pop
rock">pop
rock</a>',
although
they
have
also
experimented
and
varied
from
these
genres
at
times.<sup
id="cite_ref-Allmusic_47-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Allmusic-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>The
band's
first
four
albums
blended
the
pop
metal
and
hard
rock
genres,
although
they
had
mostly
shed
the
pop
metal
sound
by
their
fifth
studio
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Keep_the_Faith?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Keep
the
Faith">Keep
the
Faith</a></i>,
and
their
sixth,
<i><a
href="/wiki/These_Days_(Bon_Jovi_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="These
Days
(Bon
Jovi
album)">These
Days</a></i>,
utilizing
a
more
mature
hard
rock
sound.
<i><a
href="/wiki/Crush_(Bon_Jovi_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Crush
(Bon
Jovi
album)">Crush</a></i>
was
characterized
as
&quot;far
enough
into
pop/rock
to
actually
stand
a
chance
of
getting
airplay&quot;,
while
<i><a
href="/wiki/Bounce_(Bon_Jovi_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bounce
(Bon
Jovi
album)">Bounce</a></i>
was
described
as
&quot;heavy,
serious
rock&quot;.
<i><a
href="/wiki/Have_a_Nice_Day_(Bon_Jovi_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Have
a
Nice
Day
(Bon
Jovi
album)">Have
a
Nice
Day</a></i>
was
also
characterized
as
being
heavier
than
<i>Crush</i>.<sup
id="cite_ref-48"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-48"><span>[</span>48<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>The
band
altered
their
sound
dramatically
in
their
next
release,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Lost_Highway_(Bon_Jovi_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lost
Highway
(Bon
Jovi
album)">Lost
Highway</a></i>,
blending
influences
from
<a
href="/wiki/Country_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Country
music">country
music</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Country_rock?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Country
rock">country
rock</a>,
a
sound
Jon
Bon
Jovi
described
as
&quot;a
Bon
Jovi
album
influenced
by
Nashville&quot;.
Bon
Jovi
returned
to
a
more
typical
rock
sound
on
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Circle_(Bon_Jovi_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Circle
(Bon
Jovi
album)">The
Circle</a></i>,
which
was
described
by
Allmusic
as
&quot;conjured
by
echoed,
delayed
guitars,
shimmering
keyboards,
and
spacious
rhythms.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-49"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-49"><span>[</span>49<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Some
of
the
band's
influences
are
<a
href="/wiki/Bruce_Springsteen?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bruce
Springsteen">Bruce
Springsteen</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/The_Rolling_Stones?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Rolling
Stones">The
Rolling
Stones</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Aerosmith?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Aerosmith">Aerosmith</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Van_Halen?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Van
Halen">Van
Halen</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/The_Beatles?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Beatles">The
Beatles</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Tom_Petty?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tom
Petty">Tom
Petty</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/The_Animals?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Animals">The
Animals</a>.</p>

The

(2013)</li>








</ul>

<script
type="text/javascript">




render_ads(false,
window['ad_config_bot']);





function
afc_match()
{








var
count
=
-1;








if(window['ad_config_top'])
{












count
=
window['ad_config_top'];








}









var
countBottom
=
0;








if(window['ad_config_bot'])
{












countBottom
=
window['ad_config_bot'];








}









if(window['backfillParam'])
{




























window['backfillParam']['pl_bmodn']
=
5;
























window['backfillParam']['pl_tnum']
=
count;












window['backfillParam']['pl_bnum']
=
countBottom;








}


































var
_matchUrl
=
"/afc-match?q=Bon_Jovi&page=1&ac=24&qid=395DDF2CBE9E39AAC600CC507BBB01B4&qsrc=121&dm=&qrt=2&lid="+
"&o=0&l=dir&oo=&cl=ca-aj-cat&ch=cx_ask_wiki,ad_dirN";





















_matchUrl+=
"&userip=76.78.3.114";




































_matchUrl+="&losid=a&locid=encw&lodid=us&loaid=a16";









var
location
=
window.location
+
"";








location
=
location.substring(7);








var
cutIdx
=
location.indexOf("/");








if
(location.indexOf(":")
>
-1)
{




















cutIdx
=
1
+
cutIdx
+
location.substring(cutIdx+1).indexOf("/");








}









var
urlPrefix
=
location.substring(0,
cutIdx);








_matchUrl
=
"http://"
+
urlPrefix
+
_matchUrl
+
"&afcec="
+
count
+
"&afcecb="
+
countBottom;








ajax_get(_matchUrl,
null,
null);




}





function
getXHR()
{








if
(window.XMLHttpRequest)
{












return
new
XMLHttpRequest();








}
else
if
(window.ActiveXObject)
{












try
{
















return
new
ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");












}
catch
(e)
{
















try
{




















return
new
ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
















}
catch
(E)
{




















return
null;
















}












}








}








else
{












return
null;








}




}





function
ajax_get(url,
onsuccess,
onerror)
{








var
obj
=
getXHR();








if(obj)
{












obj.onreadystatechange
=
function()
{
















if(obj.readyState==4)
{




















if
(obj.status
==
200
&&
typeof(onsuccess)
==
"function")
{
























onsuccess(obj);




















}
else
if
(typeof(onerror)
==
"function")
{
























onerror(obj);




















}






















try
{
























delete
obj['onreadystatechange'];




















}
catch(e)
{}
















}












};












obj.open("GET",
url,
true,
"",
"");












obj.send(null);












return
obj;








}
else
{












if(onerror)
{
















onerror("Error
creating
XHR");












}
else
{
















a10.debug("Error
creating
XHR");












}












return
null;








}




}





afc_match();

</script>

<h2

</span>

<p
class="ur">
<span
class="grey
b

<span
class="qna-txt">
Bon
Jovi
is
47
years

His

name
is
John

};
